        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18667030-sweet-reckoning">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36178759-nicay-dearnicay?shelf=kindle">kindle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36178759-nicay-dearnicay?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1311007592" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer925511600898944117"><blockquote>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465705811i/19390951.png' width='350' height='100' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>Life was often so cruel, so ugly. And then, in the midst of all the madness, a precious gift would be placed in your lap, because life could also be so sweet.</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>It’s time for Anna to fulfill the prophecy.</b><br/><br/>The third and final book of the Sweet evil series – <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16007855.Sweet_Reckoning__The_Sweet_Trilogy___3_' title='Sweet Reckoning (The Sweet Trilogy, #3) by Wendy Higgins' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sweet Reckoning</a> by <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4279785.Wendy_Higgins' title='Wendy Higgins' rel='nofollow noopener'>Wendy Higgins</a> continued on how Anna and her Nephilim friends will expose the prophecy together with the new and still unknown allies, she was ready to face the Dukes and give what they really deserve – <i>to accept the rede</i></span>
  <span id="freeText925511600898944117" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1465705811i/19390951.png" width="350" height="100" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Life was often so cruel, so ugly. And then, in the midst of all the madness, a precious gift would be placed in your lap, because life could also be so sweet.</i>
</blockquote><br><br><b>It’s time for Anna to fulfill the prophecy.</b><br><br>The third and final book of the Sweet evil series – <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16007855.Sweet_Reckoning__The_Sweet_Trilogy___3_" title="Sweet Reckoning (The Sweet Trilogy, #3) by Wendy Higgins" rel="nofollow noopener">Sweet Reckoning</a> by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4279785.Wendy_Higgins" title="Wendy Higgins" rel="nofollow noopener">Wendy Higgins</a> continued on how Anna and her Nephilim friends will expose the prophecy together with the new and still unknown allies, she was ready to face the Dukes and give what they really deserve – <i>to accept the redemption or stay in hell.</i><br><br>But it will not be easy for them to accomplish it; there were still hindrances in their way that they didn’t know if they can win it or not.<br><br><i>
  <b>My reaction after reading this:</b>
</i><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1467462780i/19595685.gif" width="304" height="171" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/354270.gif" width="304" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452442132ra/17694575.gif" width="304" height="168" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>Oh my gosh! The story leaves me breathless and the ending was pure sweetness.<br><br>The Sweet Reckoning, the final conclusion of the book, tells what will happen for the Nephilims and for the fallen angels. The story really explodes my heart at the intense scenes and sexiness of Anna and Kaidan. From start to finish, I can’t really tear off my eyes from the book, which I imagined if I blink once there were tendency that it will gone. But, it’s just my paranoid imagination.<br><br>Their characters here really improved; they became stronger, braver and… addictive. Kaidan and Anna Whitt’s chemistry was undeniably impressive.<br><br>I honestly cried at the scene of Anna and Patti, it really broke my heart. It’s just..<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/532442.gif" width="304" height="158" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><b>I will not tell you why, discover it for yourself, baby.</b> *Smirks at the corner.<br><br>I didn’t want to finish it, but good stories must really come to end. Agree? But, you can really re-read it. LOL.<br><br><i>I will forever cherish this moment that I become a forever admirer of this book.</i><br><br><i>
  <b>Sigh for Kai.<br>Anna Whitt for the win.</b>
</i><br><br>Thank you for this lovely story Ms. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4279785.Wendy_Higgins" title="Wendy Higgins" rel="nofollow noopener">Wendy Higgins</a>. Thank you.<br><br><blockquote>
<a href="http://queennicaybooks.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Wordpress</a>┃<a href="http://instagram.com/thenerdysideofaqueen" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> ┃ <a href="http://twitter.com/queennicay" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> ┃ <a href="http://queennicay.tumblr.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a>
</blockquote><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="925511600898944117" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('dddZnKO7xnHaGxKVmL74RO5VhkUZWI+SzineKz82fEiLTcoInuMNPNDGg8nVxwJR2yYSlLxTG+X6mfR9iYhbYg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('k8UDryB4wVI2qMm0rgLnceTbBKp55UbyvU/tPjOijIBtX5A7HSAKHzx1WOjjex1k0aiQe9zu0oWJ/8dohRyrqg==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
